You can download one in the app, or from www.kiwix.org in your browser. You *must* download an archive for this app to work properly: it only comes bundled with a small test archive (about a jazz musician) so you can get a feel for how the app works.\r\n\r\nIf you want the full English-language Wikipedia with images, you will need a *large* microSD card in your device, or plenty of disk space.
